      const THEME_ID = new URLSearchParams(document.cookie.replace(/; /g, '&')).get('wdpThemeId') || 'dark2021';
      const activeTheme = THEME[THEME_ID];
      const camelCaseToKebabCase = (string) => {
        if (!string) {
          return string;
        }
        return string.replace(/([A-Z]+)/g, '-$1').toLowerCase();
      }

      let styleText = '[data-pen-theme='+THEME_ID+']{';
      for (const prop in activeTheme) {
        styleText += '--pen-'+camelCaseToKebabCase(prop)+':'+activeTheme[prop]+';';
      }
      styleText += '}';
      const style = document.createElement('style');
      style.innerText = styleText;
      style.id = 'pen-theme-'+THEME_ID;
      document.head.appendChild(style);
      document.documentElement.dataset["penTheme"] = THEME_ID;
    } catch (err) {
        console.log("Apply theme error", err);
    }

<script type="text/javascript">
      if (typeof window === 'object') {
        function getCookie(name) {
           const cookie = Object.fromEntries(new URLSearchParams(document.cookie.replace(/; /g, '&')));
           return cookie[name] || undefined;
        }
        if ("serviceWorker" in navigator) {
          navigator.serviceWorker.register("/service-worker.js", {scope: '/'})
            .then(function(reg){
              if (reg.active) console.log('serviceworker installed')

              if(navigator.serviceWorker.ready) {
                navigator.serviceWorker.ready.then(() => {
                  navigator.serviceWorker.controller.postMessage({
                    type: 'MESSAGE_UUID',
                    uuid: getCookie('uuid')
                  });
                  navigator.serviceWorker.controller.postMessage({
                    type: 'MESSAGE_STATIC_EVENTS_MAINJS_URL',
                    url: "https://log.rutube.ru/static_events",
                  });
                });
              }
            }).catch((e) => {
                console.log(e, 'navigator.serviceWorker');
            })
        }
      }

      if (typeof window === 'object') {
        if (/(^\/pl)(\/|$)/.test(window.location.pathname)) {
          let redirectUrl = window.location.origin;
          const search = window.location.search;
          const params = search.substring(1).split('&').reduce((acc, param) => {
            const [name, value] = param.split('=');
            acc[name] = value;
            return acc;
          }, { pl_id: '', pl_video: '' });
          if (params.pl_video) {
            redirectUrl += '/play/embed/' + params.pl_video;
            window.location.replace(redirectUrl);
          }
        }
      }
